    Pokemon Changes

    General Changes

    1. The Fairy-type has been added to the game, replacing the almost unused ???-type.
    2. All PokÃ©mon have had their base stats updated to match Ultra Sun and Ultra Moon.
    3. All PokÃ©mon have had their types updated to match Ultra Sun and Ultra Moon.
    4. All PokÃ©mon have had their wild held item updated to match Ultra Sun and Ultra Moon (with some exceptions).
    5. All PokÃ©mon now have an egg cycle of 0, i.e. they will hatch extremely quickly.
    6. Wingull, Pelipper and Torkoal have gained their new abilities from Gen VII.

    Held Item Exceptions

    1. PokÃ©mon who may hold an item in Ultra Sun and Ultra Moon that doesn't exist in Platinum will not hold anything.
    2. Corsola has a 5% chance to hold a Hard Stone.
    3. Pelipper has a 5% chance to hold a Lucky Egg.
    4. Absol has a 5% chance to hold a Life Orb.
    5. Spiritomb has a 100% chance to hold a Smoke Ball.

    Other Changes

    1. Some PokÃ©mon have ability slots flipped (e.g. Scyther). This is because enemy Trainers always use the first ability.

    Custom Changes

    1. From the bases as listed above, further changes to any PokÃ©mon are listed below. These can include changes to base stats, abilities, types etcetera.
    2. Any changes marked with (Complete) are only found in the Complete version. This includes all base stat and non-canon type changes (i.e. types that aren't accurate as of Gen 7), and any ability changes that give an ability to a PokÃ©mon it has never had before (e.g. Weavile). Likewise, any changes marked with (Classic) are only in found in the Classic version. All other changes are in both versions.
    3. Some PokÃ©mon have had a Hidden Ability from a later generation added as a regular ability (e.g. Ninetales). These changes are in both the Complete and Classic versions.
    4. Changes to movepools e.g. learning moves by level up or TM that were not possible before are also present in both the Complete and Classic versions.
    5. TM compatibilty with any of the new TMs (Bug Buzz, Hurricane) is also listed here.
    6. Any move previously unavailable to a PokÃ©mon is listed with a (!!) besides it.
    7. Level up moves have also been changed for every single PokÃ©mon. These should include all moves they learn in Ultra Sun and Ultra Moon that are available in Renegade Platinum, as well as additional moves from move tutors, egg moves or entirely new techniques.
    8. Each PokÃ©mon is listed under its own section header below.
